## Code Review Gate - 2026-02-28 10:16:42

🔍 **Deep Code Review:** VERDICT: APPROVE

This is a frontend-only page component — no Convex backend code here. All queries/mutations are called via `useQuery`/`useMutation` hooks (client-side), so Convex pattern rules don't apply to this file.

Minor notes:
- `console.error(error)` at line 593 is acceptable in a `catch` block (it's for debugging failed submissions, not a leftover debug log)
- All data access is scoped through `playerIdentityId` derived from the authenticated session's email
- `organizationId` is passed to mutations (`orgId` from route params) — correct pattern
- User identity uses `session?.user?.email` (not `user.id`/`user.firstName`) — correct
- Age calculation logic is duplicated (lines 396-400 and 686-688) — minor code smell but not a bug

No blocking issues found.

## PRD Audit - US-P8-007 - 2026-02-28 10:13:31
**PASS**: All criteria met.

The US-P8-007 implementation is fully verified:

1. **15-min cron** — `crons.ts:283-289` registers `check-wellness-dispatch` with `{ minutes: 15 }` interval
2. **UTC→timezone matching** — `wellnessDispatch.ts:49-100` uses `Intl.DateTimeFormat` for timezone conversion; checks 15-min window per org
3. **Per-org dispatch logic** (all sub-criteria verified):
   - Opted-in players queried via `whatsappWellness.ts:740-780` (filters `whatsappOptIn === true` and `wellnessChannel` set)
   - `dailyPlayerHealthChecks` checked via `by_player_and_date` index — skips if record found
   - `whatsapp_flows`: checks `lastFlowSentDate === dispatchDate` — skips if already sent
   - `sms_conversational`: checks `whatsappWellnessSessions` via `by_phone_and_date` index — skips if active session exists
   - `enabledDimensions` fetched via `getWellnessSettings` query
   - Dispatches through `WellnessDispatchService.sendWellnessCheck()` routing to correct channel
   - Logs sent/skipped/failed counts per batch
4. **Error handling** — `wellnessDispatch.ts:504-517`: flows failure triggers SMS fallback, logs warning, does not abort batch
5. **Rate limiting** — `DISPATCH_BATCH_SIZE = 50`, `BATCH_DELAY_MS = 60_000`, uses `ctx.scheduler.runAfter(i * BATCH_DELAY_MS, ...)` for staggered multi-batch dispatch

## PRD Audit - US-P8-009 - 2026-02-28 10:28:27
**PARTIAL: US-P8-009 — Most criteria met, two gaps remain**

**Implemented (5/7):**
- Notifications tab added to admin analytics (`analytics/page.tsx` + `whatsapp-notifications-tab.tsx`)
- Today's summary showing WhatsApp Flows sent/completed, SMS sent/completed, and skipped counts
- Channel breakdown chart (30-day stacked bar by source)
- Error log (failed dispatches, last 7 days)
- Fallback events list (WhatsApp → SMS fallbacks)

**Missing (2/7):**

1. **Player table** — No per-player monitoring table with Name, Team, Channel, Status (Sent/Completed/Abandoned/Skipped), Completion time, Score. Neither the frontend component nor backend has a query to fetch/join player-level dispatch data with names, teams, and health check scores.

2. **Not-registered section** — Shows a generic instructional message but does **not** enumerate players in target teams without a registered phone, show a count, or offer an in-app nudge button. The backend query to fetch unregistered players by team also doesn't exist.

## PRD Audit - US-P8-UAT - 2026-02-28 10:37:26
**PARTIAL**

The test file `apps/web/uat/tests/whatsapp-wellness-phase8.spec.ts` exists and covers most acceptance criteria, but several specific criteria are not met:

**What's present:**
- Test file created at the correct path ✅
- Player settings page loads, wellness section visible, phone number input/verify button present (P8-001 to P8-004) ✅
- Admin settings wellness dispatch section (P8-005, P8-006) ✅
- Health check history section renders (P8-007, P8-008) ✅
- Admin Notifications tab with dispatch summary, error log, and 30-day chart (P8-009 to P8-012) ✅
- All 16 manual test protocols documented (plus a 17th bonus WELLNESSSTOP test) ✅

**What's missing:**

1. **"UI Test: WhatsApp-available number shows 'WhatsApp Flows' channel label"** — P8-004 only loosely checks for `/whatsapp flows|sms will be used|channel/i` text without a registered WhatsApp number state. No test specifically verifies the channel label after a WhatsApp number is registered and detected.

2. **"UI Test: SMS-only number shows 'SMS' channel label"** — No test for this state at all.

3. **"UI Test: app health-check history shows WhatsApp icon for whatsapp_flows records"** — P8-008 only checks if the section renders; there is no test asserting a WhatsApp icon is displayed for `whatsapp_flows` source records.

4. **"Backend test: `getActiveWellnessSession` returns null / returns session when active"** — Entirely absent. No backend/API-level tests in the file.

5. **"Backend test: `submitDailyHealthCheck` idempotency"** — Entirely absent.
